05186 subroutine legendre_set_cos ( norder, xtab, weight )
05187 !
05188 !*******************************************************************************
05189 !
05190 !! LEGENDRE_SET_COS sets a Gauss-Legendre rule for COS(X) * F(X) on [-PI/2,PI/2].
05191 !
05192 !
05193 !  Integration interval:
05194 !
05195 !    [ -PI/2, PI/2 ]
05196 !
05197 !  Weight function:
05198 !
05199 !    COS(X) * F(X)
05200 !
05201 !  Integral to approximate:
05202 !
05203 !    Integral ( -PI/2 <= X <= PI/2 ) COS(X) * F(X) dX
05204 !
05205 !  Approximate integral:
05206 !
05207 !    Sum ( 1 <= I <= NORDER ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( XTAB(I) )
05208 !
05209 !  Discussion:
05210 !
05211 !    The same rule can be used to approximate
05212 !
05213 !      Integral ( 0 <= X <= PI ) SIN(X) * F(X) dX
05214 !
05215 !    as
05216 !
05217 !      Sum ( 1 <= I <= NORDER ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( XTAB(I) + PI/2 )
05218 !
05219 !  Reference:
05220 !
05221 !    Gwynne Evans,
05222 !    Practical Numerical Integration,
05223 !    Wiley, 1993, QA299.3E93, page 310.
05224 !
05225 !  Modified:
05226 !
05227 !    23 November 2000
05228 !
05229 !  Author:
05230 !
05231 !    John Burkardt
05232 !
05233 !  Parameters:
05234 !
05235 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.
05236 !    NORDER must be between 1, 2, 4, 8 or 16.
05237 !
05238 !    Output, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of the rule.
05239 !
05240 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
05241 !
05242   implicit none
05243 !
05244   integer norder
05245 !
05246   double precision xtab(norder)
05247   double precision weight(norder)
05248 !
05249   if ( norder == 1 ) then
05250 
05251     xtab(1) = 0.0D+00
05252 
05253     weight(1) = 2.0D+00
05254 
05255   else if ( norder == 2 ) then
05256 
05257     xtab(1) = - 0.68366739008990304094D+00
05258     xtab(2) =   0.68366739008990304094D+00
05259 
05260     weight(1) = 1.0D+00
05261     weight(2) = 1.0D+00
05262 
05263   else if ( norder == 4 ) then
05264 
05265     xtab(1) = - 1.1906765638948557415D+00
05266     xtab(2) = - 0.43928746686001514756D+00
05267     xtab(3) =   0.43928746686001514756D+00
05268     xtab(4) =   1.1906765638948557415D+00
05269 
05270     weight(1) = 0.22407061812762016065D+00
05271     weight(2) = 0.77592938187237983935D+00
05272     weight(3) = 0.77592938187237983935D+00
05273     weight(4) = 0.22407061812762016065D+00
05274 
05275   else if ( norder == 8 ) then
05276 
05277     xtab(1) = - 1.4414905401823575701D+00
05278     xtab(2) = - 1.1537256454567275850D+00
05279     xtab(3) = - 0.74346864787549244989D+00
05280     xtab(4) = - 0.25649650741623123020D+00
05281     xtab(5) =   0.25649650741623123020D+00
05282     xtab(6) =   0.74346864787549244989D+00
05283     xtab(7) =   1.1537256454567275850D+00
05284     xtab(8) =   1.4414905401823575701D+00
05285 
05286     weight(1) = 0.027535633513767011149D+00
05287     weight(2) = 0.14420409203022750950D+00
05288     weight(3) = 0.33626447785280459621D+00
05289     weight(4) = 0.49199579660320088314D+00
05290     weight(5) = 0.49199579660320088314D+00
05291     weight(6) = 0.33626447785280459621D+00
05292     weight(7) = 0.14420409203022750950D+00
05293     weight(8) = 0.027535633513767011149D+00
05294 
05295   else if ( norder == 16 ) then
05296 
05297     xtab( 1) = - 1.5327507132362304779D+00
05298     xtab( 2) = - 1.4446014873666514608D+00
05299     xtab( 3) = - 1.3097818904452936698D+00
05300     xtab( 4) = - 1.1330068786005003695D+00
05301     xtab( 5) = - 0.92027786206637096497D+00
05302     xtab( 6) = - 0.67861108097560545347D+00
05303     xtab( 7) = - 0.41577197673418943962D+00
05304     xtab( 8) = - 0.14003444424696773778D+00
05305     xtab( 9) =   0.14003444424696773778D+00
05306     xtab(10) =   0.41577197673418943962D+00
05307     xtab(11) =   0.67861108097560545347D+00
05308     xtab(12) =   0.92027786206637096497D+00
05309     xtab(13) =   1.1330068786005003695D+00
05310     xtab(14) =   1.3097818904452936698D+00
05311     xtab(15) =   1.4446014873666514608D+00
05312     xtab(16) =   1.5327507132362304779D+00
05313 
05314     weight( 1) = 0.0024194677567615628193D+00
05315     weight( 2) = 0.014115268156854008264D+00
05316     weight( 3) = 0.040437893946503669410D+00
05317     weight( 4) = 0.083026647573217742131D+00
05318     weight( 5) = 0.13834195526951273359D+00
05319     weight( 6) = 0.19741148870253455567D+00
05320     weight( 7) = 0.24763632094635522403D+00

05322     weight( 9) = 0.27661095764826050408D+00
05323     weight(10) = 0.24763632094635522403D+00
05324     weight(11) = 0.19741148870253455567D+00
05325     weight(12) = 0.13834195526951273359D+00
05326     weight(13) = 0.083026647573217742131D+00
05327     weight(14) = 0.040437893946503669410D+00
05328     weight(15) = 0.014115268156854008264D+00
05329     weight(16) = 0.0024194677567615628193D+00
05330 
05331   else
05332 
05333     write ( *, '(a)' ) ' '
05334     write ( *, '(a)' ) 'LEGENDRE_SET_COS - Fatal error!'
05335     write ( *, '(a,i6)' ) '  Illegal value of NORDER = ', norder
05336     stop
05337 
05338   end if
05339 
05340   return
05341 end
05342 subroutine legendre_set_cos2 ( norder, xtab, weight )
05343 !
05344 !*******************************************************************************
05345 !
05346 !! LEGENDRE_SET_COS2 sets a Gauss-Legendre rule for COS(X) * F(X) on [0,PI/2].
05347 !
05348 !
05349 !  Integration interval:
05350 !
05351 !    [ 0, PI/2 ]
05352 !
05353 !  Weight function:
05354 !
05355 !    COS(X) * F(X)
05356 !
05357 !  Integral to approximate:
05358 !
05359 !    Integral ( 0 <= X <= PI/2 ) COS(X) * F(X) dX
05360 !
05361 !  Approximate integral:
05362 !

05374 !
05375 !  Reference:
05376 !
05377 !    Gwynne Evans,
05378 !    Practical Numerical Integration,
05379 !    Wiley, 1993, QA299.3E93, page 311.
05380 !
05381 !  Modified:
05382 !
05383 !    24 November 2000
05384 !
05385 !  Author:
05386 !
05387 !    John Burkardt
05388 !

05390 !

05392 !    NORDER must be between 2, 4, 8 or 16.

05395 !
05396 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
05397 !

05492 subroutine legendre_set_log ( norder, xtab, weight )

05704 subroutine legendre_set_sqrtx_01 ( norder, xtab, weight )
05705 !
05706 !*******************************************************************************
05707 !
05708 !! LEGENDRE_SET_SQRTX_01 sets a Gauss-Legendre rule for SQRT(X) * F(X) on [0,1].
05709 !
05710 !
05711 !  Integration interval:
05712 !
05713 !    [ 0, 1 ]
05714 !
05715 !  Weight function:
05716 !
05717 !    SQRT ( X )
05718 !
05719 !  Integral to approximate:
05720 !
05721 !    Integral ( 0 <= X <= 1 ) SQRT ( X ) * F(X) dX =
05722 !    Integral ( 0 <= Y <= 1 ) 2 * Y**2 * F(Y**2) dY.
05723 !    (using Y = SQRT(X) )
05724 !
05725 !  Approximate integral:
05726 !
05727 !    Sum ( 1 <= I <= NORDER ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( XTAB(I) )
05728 !
05729 !  Reference:
05730 !
05731 !    Daniel Zwillinger, editor,
05732 !    CRC Standard Mathematical Tables and Formulae,
05733 !    CRC Press, 30th Edition, 2000, page 696.
05734 !
05735 !  Modified:
05736 !
05737 !    23 January 2001
05738 !
05739 !  Author:
05740 !
05741 !    John Burkardt
05742 !
05743 !  Parameters:
05744 !
05745 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.
05746 !
05747 !    Output, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of the rule.
05748 !
05749 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
05750 !
05751   implicit none
05752 !
05753   integer norder
05754 !
05755   integer norder2
05756   double precision xtab(norder)
05757   double precision xtab2(2*norder+1)
05758   double precision weight(norder)
05759   double precision weight2(2*norder+1)
05760 !
05761   norder2 = 2 * norder + 1
05762 
05763   call legendre_set ( norder2, xtab2, weight2 )
05764 
05765   xtab(1:norder) = xtab2(norder+2:2*norder+1)**2
05766   weight(1:norder) = 2.0D+00 * weight2(norder+2:2*norder+1) * xtab(1:norder)
05767 
05768   return
05769 end
05770 subroutine legendre_set_sqrtx2_01 ( norder, xtab, weight )
05771 !
05772 !*******************************************************************************
05773 !
05774 !! LEGENDRE_SET_SQRTX2_01 sets a Gauss-Legendre rule for F(X) / SQRT(X) on [0,1].
05775 !
05776 !
05777 !  Integration interval:
05778 !
05779 !    [ 0, 1 ]
05780 !
05781 !  Weight function:
05782 !
05783 !    1 / SQRT ( X )
05784 !
05785 !  Integral to approximate:
05786 !
05787 !    Integral ( 0 <= X <= 1 ) F(X) / SQRT ( X ) dX
05788 !
05789 !  Approximate integral:
05790 !
05791 !    Sum ( 1 <= I <= NORDER ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( XTAB(I) )
05792 !
05793 !  Reference:
05794 !
05795 !    Daniel Zwillinger, editor,
05796 !    CRC Standard Mathematical Tables and Formulae,
05797 !    CRC Press, 30th Edition, 2000, page 696.
05798 !
05799 !  Modified:
05800 !
05801 !    21 January 2001
05802 !
05803 !  Author:
05804 !
05805 !    John Burkardt
05806 !
05807 !  Parameters:
05808 !
05809 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.
05810 !
05811 !    Output, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of the rule.
05812 !
05813 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
05814 !
05815   implicit none
05816 !
05817   integer norder
05818 !
05819   integer norder2
05820   double precision xtab(norder)
05821   double precision xtab2(2*norder+1)
05822   double precision weight(norder)
05823   double precision weight2(2*norder+1)
05824 !
05825   norder2 = 2 * norder + 1
05826 
05827   call legendre_set ( norder2, xtab2, weight2 )
05828 
05829   xtab(1:norder) = xtab2(norder+2:2*norder+1)**2
05830   weight(1:norder) = 2.0D+00 * weight2(norder+2:2*norder+1)
05831 
05832   return
05833 end

06002 subroutine legendre_set_x1 ( norder, xtab, weight )
06003 !
06004 !*******************************************************************************
06005 !
06006 !! LEGENDRE_SET_X1 sets a Gauss-Legendre rule for ( 1 + X ) * F(X) on [-1,1].
06007 !
06008 !
06009 !  Integration interval:
06010 !
06011 !    [ -1, 1 ]
06012 !
06013 !  Weight function:
06014 !
06015 !    1 + X
06016 !
06017 !  Integral to approximate:
06018 !
06019 !    Integral ( -1 <= X <= 1 ) ( 1 + X ) * F(X) dX
06020 !
06021 !  Approximate integral:
06022 !
06023 !    Sum ( 1 <= I <= NORDER ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( XTAB(I) )
06024 !
06025 !  Reference:
06026 !
06027 !    Arthur Stroud and Don Secrest,
06028 !    Gaussian Quadrature Formulas,
06029 !    Prentice Hall, 1966, Table #3.
06030 !
06031 !  Modified:
06032 !
06033 !    18 December 2000
06034 !
06035 !  Author:
06036 !
06037 !    John Burkardt
06038 !
06039 !  Parameters:
06040 !
06041 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.
06042 !    NORDER must be between 1 and 9.
06043 !
06044 !    Output, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of the rule.
06045 !
06046 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
06047 !
06048   implicit none
06049 !
06050   integer norder
06051 !
06052   double precision xtab(norder)
06053   double precision weight(norder)
06054 !
06055   if ( norder == 1 ) then
06056

06192 subroutine legendre_set_x1_01 ( norder, xtab, weight )
06193 !
06194 !*******************************************************************************
06195 !
06196 !! LEGENDRE_SET_X1_01 sets a Gauss-Legendre rule for X * F(X) on [0,1].
06197 !
06198 !
06199 !  Integration interval:
06200 !
06201 !    [ 0, 1 ]
06202 !
06203 !  Weight function:
06204 !
06205 !    X
06206 !
06207 !  Integral to approximate:
06208 !
06209 !    Integral ( 0 <= X <= 1 ) X * F(X) dX
06210 !
06211 !  Approximate integral:
06212 !
06213 !    Sum ( 1 <= I <= NORDER ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( XTAB(I) )
06214 !
06215 !  Reference:
06216 !
06217 !    Abramowitz and Stegun,
06218 !    Handbook of Mathematical Functions,
06219 !    National Bureau of Standards, 1964, page 921.
06220 !
06221 !  Modified:
06222 !
06223 !    18 November 2000
06224 !
06225 !  Author:
06226 !
06227 !    John Burkardt
06228 !
06229 !  Parameters:
06230 !
06231 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.
06232 !    NORDER must be between 1 and 8.
06233 !
06234 !    Output, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of the rule.
06235 !
06236 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
06237 !
06238   implicit none
06239 !
06240   integer norder
06241 !
06242   double precision xtab(norder)
06243   double precision weight(norder)
06244 !
06245   if ( norder == 1 ) then

06369 !    [ -1, 1 ]

06372 !
06373 !    ( 1 + X )**2

06376 !
06377 !    Integral ( -1 <= X <= 1 ) ( 1 + X )**2 * F(X) dX

06400 !    NORDER must be between 1 and 9.

06550 subroutine legendre_set_x2_01 ( norder, xtab, weight )
06551 !
06552 !*******************************************************************************
06553 !
06554 !! LEGENDRE_SET_X2_01 sets a Gauss-Legendre rule for X**2 * F(X) on [0,1].
06555 !
06556 !
06557 !  Integration interval:
06558 !
06559 !    [ 0, 1 ]
06560 !
06561 !  Weight function:
06562 !
06563 !    X**2
06564 !
06565 !  Integral to approximate:
06566 !
06567 !    Integral ( 0 <= X <= 1 ) X*X * F(X) dX
06568 !
06569 !  Approximate integral:
06570 !
06571 !    Sum ( 1 <= I <= NORDER ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( XTAB(I) )
06572 !
06573 !  Reference:
06574 !
06575 !    Abramowitz and Stegun,
06576 !    Handbook of Mathematical Functions,
06577 !    National Bureau of Standards, 1964, page 921.
06578 !
06579 !  Modified:
06580 !
06581 !    18 November 2000
06582 !
06583 !  Author:
06584 !
06585 !    John Burkardt
06586 !
06587 !  Parameters:
06588 !
06589 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.
06590 !    NORDER must be between 1 and 8.
06591 !
06592 !    Output, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of the rule.
06593 !
06594 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
06595 !
06596   implicit none
06597 !
06598   integer norder
06599 !
06600   double precision xtab(norder)
06601   double precision weight(norder)
06602 !
06603   if ( norder == 1 ) then

06718 subroutine lobatto_set ( norder, xtab, weight )
06719 !
06720 !*******************************************************************************
06721 !
06722 !! LOBATTO_SET sets abscissas and weights for Lobatto quadrature.
06723 !
06724 !
06725 !  Integration interval:
06726 !
06727 !    [ -1, 1 ].
06728 !
06729 !  Weight function:
06730 !
06731 !    1.0D+00
06732 !
06733 !  Integral to approximate:
06734 !
06735 !    Integral ( -1 <= X <= 1 ) F(X) dX
06736 !
06737 !  Approximate integral:
06738 !
06739 !    Sum ( 1 <= I <= NORDER ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( XTAB(I) )
06740 !
06741 !  Precision:
06742 !
06743 !    The quadrature rule will integrate exactly all polynomials up to
06744 !    X**(2*NORDER-3).
06745 !
06746 !  Note:
06747 !
06748 !    The Lobatto rule is distinguished by the fact that both endpoints
06749 !    (-1 and 1) are always abscissas of the rule.
06750 !
06751 !  Reference:
06752 !
06753 !    Abramowitz and Stegun,
06754 !    Handbook of Mathematical Functions,
06755 !    National Bureau of Standards, 1964.
06756 !
06757 !    Arthur Stroud and Don Secrest,
06758 !    Gaussian Quadrature Formulas,
06759 !    Prentice Hall, 1966.
06760 !
06761 !    Daniel Zwillinger, editor,
06762 !    Standard Mathematical Tables and Formulae,
06763 !    30th Edition,
06764 !    CRC Press, 1996.
06765 !
06766 !  Modified:
06767 !
06768 !    20 September 1998
06769 !
06770 !  Author:
06771 !
06772 !    John Burkardt
06773 !
06774 !  Parameters:
06775 !
06776 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.
06777 !    NORDER must be between 2 and 20.
06778 !
06779 !    Output, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas for the rule.
06780 !
06781 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
06782 !    The weights are positive, symmetric and should sum to 2.
06783 !
06784   implicit none
06785 !
06786   integer norder
06787 !
06788   double precision xtab(norder)
06789   double precision weight(norder)
06790 !
06791   if ( norder == 2 ) then
06792 
06793     xtab(1) =  - 1.0D+00
06794     xtab(2) =    1.0D+00
06795 
06796     weight(1) =  1.0D+00
06797     weight(2) =  1.0D+00
06798 
06799   else if ( norder == 3 ) then
06800 
06801     xtab(1) =  - 1.0D+00
06802     xtab(2) =    0.0D+00
06803     xtab(3) =    1.0D+00
06804 
06805     weight(1) =  1.0D+00 / 3.0D+00
06806     weight(2) =  4.0D+00 / 3.0D+00
06807     weight(3) =  1.0D+00 / 3.0D+00
06808 
06809   else if ( norder == 4 ) then
06810 
06811     xtab(1) =  - 1.0D+00
06812     xtab(2) =  - 0.447213595499957939281834733746D+00
06813     xtab(3) =    0.447213595499957939281834733746D+00
06814     xtab(4) =    1.0D+00
06815 
06816     weight(1) =  1.0D+00 / 6.0D+00
06817     weight(2) =  5.0D+00 / 6.0D+00
06818     weight(3) =  5.0D+00 / 6.0D+00
06819     weight(4) =  1.0D+00 / 6.0D+00
06820 
06821   else if ( norder == 5 ) then
06822 
06823     xtab(1) =  - 1.0D+00
06824     xtab(2) =  - 0.654653670707977143798292456247D+00
06825     xtab(3) =    0.0D+00
06826     xtab(4) =    0.654653670707977143798292456247D+00
06827     xtab(5) =    1.0D+00

06833     weight(5) =  9.0D+00 / 90.0D+00

07297 function log_gamma ( x )
07298 !
07299 !*******************************************************************************
07300 !
07301 !! LOG_GAMMA calculates the natural logarithm of GAMMA(X).
07302 !
07303 !
07304 !  Discussion:
07305 !
07306 !    The method uses Stirling's approximation, and is accurate to about
07307 !    12 decimal places.
07308 !
07309 !  Reference:
07310 !
07311 !    Arthur Stroud and Don Secrest,
07312 !    Gaussian Quadrature Formulas,
07313 !    Prentice Hall, 1966.
07314 !
07315 !  Modified:
07316 !
07317 !    19 September 1998
07318 !
07319 !  Parameters:
07320 !
07321 !    Input, double precision X, the evaluation point.  The routine
07322 !    will fail if GAMMA(X) is not positive.  X should be greater than 0.
07323 !
07324 !    Output, double precision LOG_GAMMA, the natural logarithm of the
07325 !    gamma function of X.
07326 !
07327   implicit none
07328 !
07329   double precision d_pi
07330   integer i
07331   integer k
07332   double precision log_gamma
07333   integer m
07334   double precision p
07335   double precision x
07336   double precision x2
07337   double precision y
07338   double precision z
07339 !
07340   if ( x < 0.5 ) then
07341 
07342     m = 1
07343     x2 = 1.0D+00 - x
07344 
07345   else
07346 
07347     m = 0
07348     x2 = x
07349 
07350   end if
07351 
07352   k = - 1
07353 
07354   do
07355 
07356     k = k + 1
07357 
07358     if ( x2 + dble ( k ) > 6.0D+00 ) then
07359       exit
07360     end if
07361 
07362   end do
07363 
07364   z = x2 + dble ( k )
07365 
07366   y = ( z - 0.5 ) * log ( z ) - z + 0.9189385332047D+00 + &
07367        ( ( ( ( ( &
07368        - 4146.0D+00 / z**2 &
07369        + 1820.0D+00 ) / z**2 &
07370        - 1287.0D+00 ) / z**2 &
07371        + 1716.0D+00 ) / z**2 &
07372        - 6006.0D+00 ) / z**2 &
07373        + 180180.0D+00 ) / z / 2162160.0D+00
07374 
07375   if ( k > 0 ) then
07376 
07377     do i = 1, k
07378       y = y - log ( x2 + dble ( k - i ) )
07379     end do
07380 
07381   end if
07382 
07383   if ( m /= 0 ) then
07384 
07385     p = d_pi ( ) / sin ( d_pi ( ) * ( 1.0D+00 - x2 ) )
07386 
07387     if ( p <= 0.0D+00 ) then
07388 
07389       write ( *, '(a)' ) ' '
07390       write ( *, '(a)' ) 'LOG_GAMMA - fatal error!'
07391       stop
07392 
07393     else
07394 
07395       y = log ( p ) - y
07396 
07397     end if
07398 
07399   end if
07400 
07401   log_gamma = y
07402 
07403   return
07404 end
07405 subroutine moulton_set ( norder, xtab, weight )
07406 !
07407 !*******************************************************************************
07408 !
07409 !! MOULTON_SET sets weights for Adams-Moulton quadrature.
07410 !
07411 !
07412 !  Definition:
07413 !
07414 !    Adams-Moulton quadrature formulas are normally used in solving
07415 !    ordinary differential equations, and are not suitable for general
07416 !    quadrature computations.  However, an Adams-Moulton formula is
07417 !    equivalent to approximating the integral of F(Y(X)) between X(M)
07418 !    and X(M+1), using an implicit formula that relies on known values
07419 !    of F(Y(X)) at X(M-N+1) through X(M), plus the unknown value at X(M+1).
07420 !
07421 !    Suppose the unknown function is denoted by Y(X), with derivative F(Y(X)),
07422 !    and that approximate values of the function are known at a series of
07423 !    X values, which we write as X(1), X(2), ..., X(M).  We write the value
07424 !    Y(X(1)) as Y(1) and so on.
07425 !
07426 !    Then the solution of the ODE Y' = F(X,Y) at the next point X(M+1) is
07427 !    computed by:
07428 !
07429 !      Y(M+1) = Y(M) + Integral ( X(M) < X < X(M+1) ) F(Y(X)) dX
07430 !             = Y(M) + H * Sum ( I = 1 to N ) W(I) * F(Y(M+2-I)) approximately.
07431 !
07432 !    Note that this formula is implicit, since the unknown value Y(M+1)
07433 !    appears on the right hand side.  Hence, in ODE applications, this
07434 !    equation must be solved via a nonlinear equation solver.  For
07435 !    quadrature problems, where the function to be integrated is known
07436 !    beforehand, this is not a problem, and the calculation is explicit.
07437 !
07438 !    In the documentation that follows, we replace F(Y(X)) by F(X).
07439 !
07440 !  Integration interval:
07441 !
07442 !    [ 0, 1 ]
07443 !
07444 !  Weight function:
07445 !
07446 !    1.0D+00
07447 !
07448 !  Integral to approximate:
07449 !
07450 !    Integral ( 0 <= X <= 1 ) F(X) dX
07451 !
07452 !  Approximate integral:
07453 !
07454 !    Sum ( 1 <= I <= NORDER ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( 2 - I )
07455 !
07456 !  Note:
07457 !
07458 !    The Adams-Moulton formulas require equally spaced data.
07459 !
07460 !    Here is how the formula is applied in the case with non-unit spacing:
07461 !
07462 !      Integral ( A <= X <= A+H ) F(X) dX =
07463 !      H * Sum ( 1 <= I <= NORDER ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( A - (I-2)*H ), approximately.
07464 !
07465 !  Reference:
07466 !
07467 !    Abramowitz and Stegun,
07468 !    Handbook of Mathematical Functions,
07469 !    National Bureau of Standards, 1964,
07470 !    page 915 ("Lagrangian Integration Coefficients").
07471 !
07472 !    Jean Lapidus and John Seinfeld,
07473 !    Numerical Solution of Ordinary Differential Equations,
07474 !    Academic Press, 1971.
07475 !
07476 !    Daniel Zwillinger, editor,
07477 !    Standard Mathematical Tables and Formulae,
07478 !    30th Edition,
07479 !    CRC Press, 1996.
07480 !
07481 !  Modified:
07482 !
07483 !    16 September 1998
07484 !
07485 !  Author:
07486 !
07487 !    John Burkardt
07488 !
07489 !  Parameters:
07490 !
07491 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.  NORDER must be
07492 !    between 1 and 10.
07493 !
07494 !    Output, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of the rule.
07495 !
07496 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
07497 !    WEIGHT(1) is the weight at X = 1, WEIGHT(2) the weight at X = 0, and so on.
07498 !    The weights are rational.  The weights are not symmetric, and
07499 !    some weights may be negative.  They should sum to 1.
07500 !
07501   implicit none
07502 !
07503   integer norder
07504 !
07505   double precision d
07506   integer i
07507   double precision weight(norder)
07508   double precision xtab(norder)
07509 !
07510   if ( norder == 1 ) then
07511 
07512     weight(1) =  1.0D+00
07513 
07514   else if ( norder == 2 ) then
07515 
07516     d = 2.0D+00
07517 
07518     weight(1) =  1.0D+00 / d
07519     weight(2) =  1.0D+00 / d
07520 
07521   else if ( norder == 3 ) then
07522 
07523     d = 12.0D+00
07524 
07525     weight(1) =    5.0D+00 / d
07526     weight(2) =    8.0D+00 / d
07527     weight(3) =  - 1.0D+00 / d
07528 
07529   else if ( norder == 4 ) then
07530 
07531     d = 24.0D+00
07532 
07533     weight(1) =    9.0D+00 / d
07534     weight(2) =   19.0D+00 / d
07535     weight(3) =  - 5.0D+00 / d
07536     weight(4) =    1.0D+00 / d
07537 
07538   else if ( norder == 5 ) then
07539 
07540     d = 720.0D+00
07541 
07542     weight(1) =    251.0D+00 / d
07543     weight(2) =    646.0D+00 / d
07544     weight(3) =  - 264.0D+00 / d
07545     weight(4) =    106.0D+00 / d
07546     weight(5) =   - 19.0D+00 / d
07547 
07548   else if ( norder == 6 ) then
07549 
07550     d = 1440.0D+00
07551 
07552     weight(1) =    475.0D+00 / d
07553     weight(2) =   1427.0D+00 / d
07554     weight(3) =  - 798.0D+00 / d
07555     weight(4) =    482.0D+00 / d
07556     weight(5) =  - 173.0D+00 / d
07557     weight(6) =     27.0D+00 / d
07558 
07559   else if ( norder == 7 ) then
07560 
07561     d = 60480.0D+00
07562 
07563     weight(1) =    19087.0D+00 / d
07564     weight(2) =    65112.0D+00 / d
07565     weight(3) =  - 46461.0D+00 / d
07566     weight(4) =    37504.0D+00 / d
07567     weight(5) =  - 20211.0D+00 / d
07568     weight(6) =     6312.0D+00 / d
07569     weight(7) =    - 863.0D+00 / d
07570 
07571   else if ( norder == 8 ) then
07572 
07573     d = 120960.0D+00
07574 
07575     weight(1) =    36799.0D+00 / d
07576     weight(2) =   139849.0D+00 / d
07577     weight(3) = - 121797.0D+00 / d
07578     weight(4) =   123133.0D+00 / d
07579     weight(5) =  - 88547.0D+00 / d
07580     weight(6) =    41499.0D+00 / d
07581     weight(7) =  - 11351.0D+00 / d
07582     weight(8) =     1375.0D+00 / d
07583 
07584   else if ( norder == 9 ) then
07585 
07586     d = 3628800.0D+00
07587 
07588     weight(1) =   1070017.0D+00 / d
07589     weight(2) =   4467094.0D+00 / d
07590     weight(3) = - 4604594.0D+00 / d
07591     weight(4) =   5595358.0D+00 / d
07592     weight(5) = - 5033120.0D+00 / d
07593     weight(6) =   3146338.0D+00 / d
07594     weight(7) = - 1291214.0D+00 / d
07595     weight(8) =    312874.0D+00 / d
07596     weight(9) =   - 33953.0D+00 / d
07597 
07598   else if ( norder == 10 ) then
07599 
07600     d = 7257600.0D+00
07601 
07602     weight(1) =    2082753.0D+00 / d
07603     weight(2) =    9449717.0D+00 / d
07604     weight(3) = - 11271304.0D+00 / d
07605     weight(4) =   16002320.0D+00 / d
07606     weight(5) = - 17283646.0D+00 / d
07607     weight(6) =   13510082.0D+00 / d
07608     weight(7) =  - 7394032.0D+00 / d
07609     weight(8) =    2687864.0D+00 / d
07610     weight(9) =   - 583435.0D+00 / d
07611     weight(10) =     57281.0D+00 / d
07612 
07613   else
07614 
07615     write ( *, '(a)' ) ' '
07616     write ( *, '(a)' ) 'MOULTON_SET - Fatal error!'
07617     write ( *, '(a,i6)' ) '  Illegal value of NORDER = ', norder
07618     write ( *, '(a)' ) '  Legal values are 1 through 10.'
07619     stop
07620 
07621   end if
07622 
07623   do i = 1, norder
07624     xtab(i) = dble ( 2 - i )
07625   end do
07626 
07627   return
07628 end
07629 subroutine ncc_com ( norder, xtab, weight )
07630 !
07631 !*******************************************************************************
07632 !
07633 !! NCC_COM computes the coefficients of a Newton-Cotes closed quadrature rule.
07634 !
07635 !
07636 !  Definition:
07637 !
07638 !    For the interval [-1,1], the Newton-Cotes open quadrature rule
07639 !    estimates
07640 !
07641 !      Integral ( -1 <= X <= 1 ) F(X) dX
07642 !
07643 !    using NORDER equally spaced abscissas XTAB(I) and a weight vector
07644 !    WEIGHT(I):
07645 !
07646 !      Sum ( I = 1 to N ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( XTAB(I) ).
07647 !
07648 !    For the CLOSED rule, the abscissas include A and B.
07649 !
07650 !  Modified:
07651 !
07652 !    25 September 1998
07653 !
07654 !  Author:
07655 !
07656 !    John Burkardt
07657 !
07658 !  Parameters:
07659 !
07660 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule, which should be
07661 !    at least 2.
07662 !
07663 !    Output, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of the rule.
07664 !
07665 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
07666 !
07667   implicit none
07668 !
07669   integer norder
07670 !
07671   double precision a
07672   double precision b
07673   integer i
07674   double precision weight(norder)
07675   double precision xtab(norder)
07676 !
07677 !  Compute a closed quadrature rule.
07678 !
07679   a = -1.0D+00
07680   b =  1.0D+00
07681 
07682   if ( norder == 1 ) then
07683 
07684     xtab(1) = 0.0D+00
07685     weight(1) = 2.0D+00
07686     return
07687 
07688   else
07689 
07690     do i = 1, norder
07691       xtab(i) = ( dble ( norder - i ) * a + dble ( i - 1 ) * b ) / &
07692         dble ( norder - 1 )
07693     end do
07694 
07695   end if
07696 
07697   call nc_com ( norder, a, b, xtab, weight )
07698 
07699   return
07700 end
07701 subroutine nc_com ( norder, a, b, xtab, weight )
07702 !
07703 !*******************************************************************************
07704 !
07705 !! NC_COM computes the coefficients of a Newton-Cotes quadrature rule.
07706 !
07707 !
07708 !  Definition:
07709 !
07710 !    For the interval [A,B], the Newton-Cotes quadrature rule estimates
07711 !
07712 !      Integral ( A <= X <= B ) F(X) dX
07713 !
07714 !    using NORDER equally spaced abscissas XTAB(I) and a weight vector
07715 !    WEIGHT(I):
07716 !
07717 !      Sum ( I = 1 to N ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( XTAB(I) ).
07718 !
07719 !    For the CLOSED rule, the abscissas include the points A and B.
07720 !    For the OPEN rule, the abscissas do not include A and B.
07721 !
07722 !  Modified:
07723 !
07724 !    25 September 1998
07725 !
07726 !  Author:
07727 !
07728 !    John Burkardt
07729 !
07730 !  Parameters:
07731 !
07732 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.
07733 !
07734 !    Input, double precision A, B, the left and right endpoints of the interval
07735 !    over which the quadrature rule is to be applied.
07736 !
07737 !    Input, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of the rule.
07738 !
07739 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
07740 !
07741   implicit none
07742 !
07743   integer norder
07744 !
07745   double precision a
07746   double precision b
07747   double precision diftab(norder)
07748   integer i
07749   integer j
07750   integer k
07751   double precision weight(norder)
07752   double precision xtab(norder)
07753   double precision yvala
07754   double precision yvalb
07755 !
07756   do i = 1, norder
07757 !
07758 !  Compute the Lagrange basis polynomial which is 1 at XTAB(I),
07759 !  and zero at the other nodes.
07760 !
07761     diftab(1:norder) = 0.0D+00
07762     diftab(i) = 1.0D+00
07763 
07764     do j = 2, norder
07765       do k = j, norder
07766         diftab(norder+j-k) = ( diftab(norder+j-k-1) - diftab(norder+j-k) ) &
07767           / ( xtab(norder+1-k) - xtab(norder+j-k) )
07768       end do
07769     end do
07770 
07771     do j = 1, norder-1
07772       do k = 1, norder-j
07773         diftab(norder-k) = diftab(norder-k) - xtab(norder-k-j+1) * &
07774           diftab(norder-k+1)
07775       end do
07776     end do
07777 !
07778 !  Evaluate the antiderivative of the polynomial at the left and
07779 !  right endpoints.
07780 !
07781     yvala = diftab(norder) / dble ( norder )
07782     do j = norder-1, 1, -1
07783       yvala = yvala * a + diftab(j) / dble ( j )
07784     end do
07785     yvala = yvala * a
07786 
07787     yvalb = diftab(norder) / dble ( norder )
07788     do j = norder-1, 1, -1
07789       yvalb = yvalb * b + diftab(j) / dble ( j )
07790     end do
07791     yvalb = yvalb * b
07792 
07793     weight(i) = yvalb - yvala
07794 
07795   end do
07796 
07797   return
07798 end
07799 subroutine ncc_set ( norder, xtab, weight )
07800 !
07801 !*******************************************************************************
07802 !
07803 !! NCC_SET sets abscissas and weights for closed Newton-Cotes quadrature.
07804 !
07805 !
07806 !  Integration interval:
07807 !
07808 !    [ -1, 1 ]
07809 !
07810 !  Weight function:
07811 !
07812 !    1.0D+00
07813 !
07814 !  Integral to approximate:
07815 !
07816 !    Integral ( -1 <= X <= 1 ) F(X) dX
07817 !
07818 !  Approximate integral:
07819 !
07820 !    Sum ( 1 <= I <= NORDER ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( XTAB(I) )
07821 !
07822 !  Note:
07823 !
07824 !    The closed Newton-Cotes rules use equally spaced abscissas, and
07825 !    hence may be used with tabulated function data.
07826 !
07827 !    The rules are called "closed" because they include the endpoints.
07828 !
07829 !    The higher order rules involve negative weights.  These can produce
07830 !    loss of accuracy due to the subtraction of large, nearly equal quantities.
07831 !
07832 !    NORDER = 2 is the trapezoidal rule.
07833 !    NORDER = 3 is Simpson's rule.
07834 !    NORDER = 4 is Simpson's 3/8 rule.
07835 !    NORDER = 5 is Bode's rule.
07836 !
07837 !    The Kopal reference for NORDER = 12 lists
07838 !      WEIGHT(6) = 15494566.0D+00 / 43545600.0D+00
07839 !    but this results in a set of coeffients that don't add up to 2.
07840 !    The correct value is
07841 !      WEIGHT(6) = 15493566.0D+00 / 43545600.0.
07842 !
07843 !  Reference:
07844 !
07845 !    Abramowitz and Stegun,
07846 !    Handbook of Mathematical Functions,
07847 !    National Bureau of Standards, 1964.
07848 !
07849 !    Johnson,
07850 !    Quarterly Journal of Mathematics,
07851 !    Volume 46, Number 52, 1915.
07852 !
07853 !    Zdenek Kopal,
07854 !    Numerical Analysis,
07855 !    John Wiley, 1955.
07856 !
07857 !    Daniel Zwillinger, editor,
07858 !    Standard Mathematical Tables and Formulae,
07859 !    30th Edition,
07860 !    CRC Press, 1996.
07861 !
07862 !  Modified:
07863 !
07864 !    16 September 1998
07865 !
07866 !  Author:
07867 !
07868 !    John Burkardt
07869 !
07870 !  Parameters:
07871 !
07872 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.
07873 !    NORDER must be between 2 and 20.
07874 !
07875 !    Output, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of the rule.
07876 !    The abscissas are uniformly spaced in the interval, and include
07877 !    -1 and 1.
07878 !
07879 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
07880 !    The weights are symmetric, rational, and should sum to 2.0.
07881 !    Some weights may be negative.
07882 !
07883   implicit none
07884 !
07885   integer norder
07886 !
07887   double precision d
07888   integer i
07889   double precision weight(norder)
07890   double precision xtab(norder)
07891 !
07892   if ( norder == 2 ) then
07893 
07894     weight(1) = 1.0D+00
07895     weight(2) = 1.0D+00
07896 
07897   else if ( norder == 3 ) then
07898 
07899     d = 3.0D+00
07900 
07901     weight(1) = 1.0D+00 / d
07902     weight(2) = 4.0D+00 / d
07903     weight(3) = 1.0D+00 / d
07904 
07905   else if ( norder == 4 ) then
07906 
07907     d = 4.0D+00
07908 
07909     weight(1) = 1.0D+00 / d
07910     weight(2) = 3.0D+00 / d
07911     weight(3) = 3.0D+00 / d
07912     weight(4) = 1.0D+00 / d
07913 
07914   else if ( norder == 5 ) then
07915 
07916     d = 45.0D+00
07917 
07918     weight(1) =  7.0D+00 / d
07919     weight(2) = 32.0D+00 / d
07920     weight(3) = 12.0D+00 / d
07921     weight(4) = 32.0D+00 / d
07922     weight(5) =  7.0D+00 / d
07923 
07924   else if ( norder == 6 ) then
07925 
07926     d = 144.0D+00
07927 
07928     weight(1) = 19.0D+00 / d
07929     weight(2) = 75.0D+00 / d
07930     weight(3) = 50.0D+00 / d
07931     weight(4) = 50.0D+00 / d
07932     weight(5) = 75.0D+00 / d
07933     weight(6) = 19.0D+00 / d
07934 
07935   else if ( norder == 7 ) then
07936 
07937     d = 420.0D+00
07938 
07939     weight(1) =  41.0D+00 / d
07940     weight(2) = 216.0D+00 / d
07941     weight(3) =  27.0D+00 / d
07942     weight(4) = 272.0D+00 / d
07943     weight(5) =  27.0D+00 / d
07944     weight(6) = 216.0D+00 / d
07945     weight(7) =  41.0D+00 / d
07946 
07947   else if ( norder == 8 ) then
07948 
07949     d = 8640.0D+00
07950 
07951     weight(1) =  751.0D+00 / d
07952     weight(2) = 3577.0D+00 / d
07953     weight(3) = 1323.0D+00 / d
07954     weight(4) = 2989.0D+00 / d
07955     weight(5) = 2989.0D+00 / d
07956     weight(6) = 1323.0D+00 / d
07957     weight(7) = 3577.0D+00 / d
07958     weight(8) =  751.0D+00 / d
07959 
07960   else if ( norder == 9 ) then
07961 
07962     d = 14175.0D+00
07963 
07964     weight(1) =    989.0D+00 / d
07965     weight(2) =   5888.0D+00 / d
07966     weight(3) =  - 928.0D+00 / d
07967     weight(4) =  10496.0D+00 / d
07968     weight(5) = - 4540.0D+00 / d
07969     weight(6) =  10496.0D+00 / d
07970     weight(7) =  - 928.0D+00 / d
07971     weight(8) =   5888.0D+00 / d
07972     weight(9) =    989.0D+00 / d
07973 
07974   else if ( norder == 10 ) then
07975 
07976     d = 44800.0D+00
07977 
07978     weight(1) =   2857.0D+00 / d
07979     weight(2) =  15741.0D+00 / d
07980     weight(3) =   1080.0D+00 / d
07981     weight(4) =  19344.0D+00 / d
07982     weight(5) =   5778.0D+00 / d
07983     weight(6) =   5778.0D+00 / d
07984     weight(7) =  19344.0D+00 / d
07985     weight(8) =   1080.0D+00 / d
07986     weight(9) =  15741.0D+00 / d
07987     weight(10) =  2857.0D+00 / d
07988 
07989   else if ( norder == 11 ) then
07990 
07991     d = 299376.0D+00
07992 
07993     weight(1) =     16067.0D+00 / d
07994     weight(2) =    106300.0D+00 / d
07995     weight(3) =   - 48525.0D+00 / d
07996     weight(4) =    272400.0D+00 / d
07997     weight(5) =  - 260550.0D+00 / d

08211 end
08212 subroutine nco_com ( norder, xtab, weight )
08213 !
08214 !*******************************************************************************
08215 !
08216 !! NCO_COM computes the coefficients of a Newton-Cotes open quadrature rule.
08217 !
08218 !
08219 !  Definition:
08220 !
08221 !    For the interval [-1,1], the Newton-Cotes open quadrature rule
08222 !    estimates
08223 !
08224 !      Integral ( -1 <= X <= 1 ) F(X) dX
08225 !
08226 !    using NORDER equally spaced abscissas XTAB(I) and a weight vector
08227 !    WEIGHT(I):
08228 !
08229 !      Sum ( I = 1 to N ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( XTAB(I) ).
08230 !
08231 !    For the OPEN rule, the abscissas do not include A and B.
08232 !
08233 !  Modified:
08234 !
08235 !    25 September 1998
08236 !
08237 !  Author:
08238 !
08239 !    John Burkardt
08240 !
08241 !  Parameters:
08242 !
08243 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.
08244 !
08245 !    Output, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of the rule.
08246 !
08247 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the  rule.
08248 !
08249   implicit none
08250 !
08251   integer norder
08252 !
08253   double precision a
08254   double precision b
08255   integer i
08256   double precision weight(norder)
08257   double precision xtab(norder)
08258 !
08259   a = -1.0D+00
08260   b =  1.0D+00
08261 
08262   do i = 1, norder
08263     xtab(i) = ( dble ( norder + 1 - i ) * a + dble ( i ) * b ) &
08264       / dble ( norder + 1 )
08265   end do
08266 
08267   call nc_com ( norder, a, b, xtab, weight )
08268 
08269   return
08270 end
08271 subroutine nco_set ( norder, xtab, weight )
08272 !
08273 !*******************************************************************************
08274 !
08275 !! NCO_SET sets abscissas and weights for open Newton-Cotes quadrature.
08276 !
08277 !
08278 !  Integration interval:
08279 !
08280 !    [ -1, 1 ]
08281 !
08282 !  Weight function:
08283 !
08284 !    1.0D+00
08285 !
08286 !  Integral to approximate:
08287 !
08288 !    Integral ( -1 <= X <= 1 ) F(X) dX
08289 !
08290 !  Approximate integral:
08291 !
08292 !    Sum ( 1 <= I <= NORDER ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( XTAB(I) )
08293 !
08294 !  Note:
08295 !
08296 !    The open Newton-Cotes rules use equally spaced abscissas, and
08297 !    hence may be used with equally spaced data.
08298 !
08299 !    The rules are called "open" because they do not include the interval
08300 !    endpoints.
08301 !
08302 !    Most of the rules involve negative weights.  These can produce loss
08303 !    of accuracy due to the subtraction of large, nearly equal quantities.
08304 !
08305 !  Reference:
08306 !
08307 !    Abramowitz and Stegun,
08308 !    Handbook of Mathematical Functions,
08309 !    National Bureau of Standards, 1964.
08310 !
08311 !    Daniel Zwillinger, editor,
08312 !    Standard Mathematical Tables and Formulae,
08313 !    30th Edition,
08314 !    CRC Press, 1996.
08315 !
08316 !  Modified:
08317 !
08318 !    15 September 1998
08319 !
08320 !  Author:
08321 !
08322 !    John Burkardt
08323 !
08324 !  Parameters:
08325 !
08326 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.
08327 !    NORDER must be between 1 and 7, and 9.
08328 !
08329 !    Output, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of the rule.
08330 !
08331 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
08332 !    The weights are rational, symmetric, and should sum to 2.
08333 !    Some weights may be negative.
08334 !
08335   implicit none
08336 !
08337   integer norder
08338 !
08339   double precision d
08340   integer i
08341   double precision weight(norder)
08342   double precision xtab(norder)
08343 !
08344   if ( norder == 1 ) then
08345 
08346     weight(1) = 2.0D+00
08347 
08348   else if ( norder == 2 ) then
08349 
08350     weight(1) = 1.0D+00
08351     weight(2) = 1.0D+00
08352 
08353   else if ( norder == 3 ) then
08354 
08355     d = 3.0D+00
08356 
08357     weight(1) =   4.0D+00 / d
08358     weight(2) = - 2.0D+00 / d
08359     weight(3) =   4.0D+00 / d
08360 
08361   else if ( norder == 4 ) then
08362 
08363     d = 12.0D+00
08364 
08365     weight(1) = 11.0D+00 / d
08366     weight(2) =  1.0D+00 / d
08367     weight(3) =  1.0D+00 / d
08368     weight(4) = 11.0D+00 / d
08369 
08370   else if ( norder == 5 ) then
08371 
08372     d = 10.0D+00
08373 
08374     weight(1) =   11.0D+00 / d
08375     weight(2) = - 14.0D+00 / d
08376     weight(3) =   26.0D+00 / d
08377     weight(4) = - 14.0D+00 / d
08378     weight(5) =   11.0D+00 / d
08379 
08380   else if ( norder == 6 ) then
08381 
08382     d = 1440.0D+00
08383 
08384     weight(1) =  1222.0D+00 / d
08385     weight(2) = - 906.0D+00 / d
08386     weight(3) =  1124.0D+00 / d
08387     weight(4) =  1124.0D+00 / d
08388     weight(5) = - 906.0D+00 / d
08389     weight(6) =  1222.0D+00 / d
08390 
08391   else if ( norder == 7 ) then
08392 
08393     d = 945.0D+00
08394 
08395     weight(1) =    920.0D+00 / d
08396     weight(2) = - 1908.0D+00 / d
08397     weight(3) =   4392.0D+00 / d
08398     weight(4) = - 4918.0D+00 / d
08399     weight(5) =   4392.0D+00 / d
08400     weight(6) = - 1908.0D+00 / d
08401     weight(7) =    920.0D+00 / d
08402 
08403   else if ( norder == 9 ) then
08404 
08405     d = 4536.0D+00
08406 
08407     weight(1) =    4045.0D+00 / d
08408     weight(2) = - 11690.0D+00 / d
08409     weight(3) =   33340.0D+00 / d
08410     weight(4) = - 55070.0D+00 / d
08411     weight(5) =   67822.0D+00 / d
08412     weight(6) = - 55070.0D+00 / d
08413     weight(7) =   33340.0D+00 / d
08414     weight(8) = - 11690.0D+00 / d
08415     weight(9) =    4045.0D+00 / d
08416 
08417   else
08418 
08419     write ( *, '(a)' ) ' '
08420     write ( *, '(a)' ) 'NCO_SET - Fatal error!'
08421     write ( *, '(a,i6)' ) '  Illegal value of NORDER = ', norder
08422     write ( *, '(a)' ) '  Legal values are 1 to 7, and 9.'
08423     stop
08424 
08425   end if
08426 !
08427 !  Set the abscissas.
08428 !
08429   do i = 1, norder
08430     xtab(i) = dble ( 2 * i - norder - 1 ) / dble ( norder + 1 )
08431   end do
08432 
08433   return
08434 end
08435 function r_pi ( )
08436 !
08437 !*******************************************************************************
08438 !
08439 !! R_PI returns the value of pi as a real quantity.
08440 !
08441 !
08442 !  Modified:
08443 !
08444 !    28 April 2000
08445 !
08446 !  Author:
08447 !
08448 !    John Burkardt
08449 !
08450 !  Parameters:
08451 !
08452 !    Output, real PI, the value of pi.
08453 !
08454   implicit none
08455 !
08456   real r_pi
08457 !
08458   r_pi = 3.14159265358979323846264338327950288419716939937510E+00
08459 
08460   return
08461 end
08462 subroutine radau_set ( norder, xtab, weight )
08463 !
08464 !*******************************************************************************
08465 !
08466 !! RADAU_SET sets abscissas and weights for Radau quadrature.
08467 !
08468 !
08469 !  Integration interval:
08470 !
08471 !    [ -1, 1 ]
08472 !
08473 !  Weight function:
08474 !
08475 !    1.0D+00
08476 !
08477 !  Integral to approximate:
08478 !
08479 !    Integral ( -1 <= X <= 1 ) F(X) dX
08480 !
08481 !  Approximate integral:
08482 !
08483 !    Sum ( 1 <= I <= NORDER ) WEIGHT(I) * F ( XTAB(I) )
08484 !
08485 !  Precision:
08486 !
08487 !    The quadrature rule will integrate exactly all polynomials up to
08488 !    X**(2*NORDER-2).
08489 !
08490 !  Note:
08491 !
08492 !    The Radau rule is distinguished by the fact that the left endpoint
08493 !    (-1) is always an abscissa.
08494 !
08495 !  Reference:
08496 !
08497 !    Abramowitz and Stegun,
08498 !    Handbook of Mathematical Functions,
08499 !    National Bureau of Standards, 1964.
08500 !
08501 !    Arthur Stroud and Don Secrest,
08502 !    Gaussian Quadrature Formulas,
08503 !    Prentice Hall, 1966.
08504 !
08505 !    Daniel Zwillinger, editor,
08506 !    Standard Mathematical Tables and Formulae,
08507 !    30th Edition,
08508 !    CRC Press, 1996.
08509 !
08510 !  Modified:
08511 !
08512 !    16 September 1998
08513 !
08514 !  Author:
08515 !
08516 !    John Burkardt
08517 !
08518 !  Parameters:
08519 !
08520 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.
08521 !    NORDER must be between 1 and 15.
08522 !
08523 !    Output, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of the rule.
08524 !
08525 !    Output, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
08526 !    The weights are positive.  The weights are not symmetric.
08527 !    The weights should sum to 2.  WEIGHT(1) should equal 2 / NORDER**2.
08528 !
08529   implicit none
08530 !
08531   integer norder
08532 !
08533   double precision xtab(norder)
08534   double precision weight(norder)
08535 !
08536   if ( norder == 1 ) then
08537 
08538     xtab(1) =   - 1.0D+00
08539     weight(1) =   2.0D+00
08540 
08541   else if ( norder == 2 ) then
08542 
08543     xtab(1) =  - 1.0D+00
08544     xtab(2) =    1.0D+00 / 3.0D+00
08545 
08546     weight(1) =  0.5D+00
08547     weight(2) =  1.5D+00
08548 
08549   else if ( norder == 3 ) then
08550 
08551     xtab(1) =   - 1.0D+00
08552     xtab(2) =   - 0.289897948556635619639456814941D+00
08553     xtab(3) =     0.689897948556635619639456814941D+00
08554 
08555     weight(1) =  0.222222222222222222222222222222D+00
08556     weight(2) =  0.102497165237684322767762689304D+01
08557     weight(3) =  0.752806125400934550100150884739D+00
08558 
08559   else if ( norder == 4 ) then
08560 
08561     xtab(1) =  - 1.0D+00
08562     xtab(2) =  - 0.575318923521694112050483779752D+00
08563     xtab(3) =    0.181066271118530578270147495862D+00
08564     xtab(4) =    0.822824080974592105208907712461D+00

08847 subroutine rule_adjust ( a, b, c, d, norder, x, w )
08848 !
08849 !*******************************************************************************
08850 !
08851 !! RULE_ADJUST maps a quadrature rule from [A,B] to [C,D].
08852 !
08853 !
08854 !  Discussion:
08855 !
08856 !    Most quadrature rules are defined on a special interval, like
08857 !    [-1,1] or [0,1].  To integrate over an interval, the abscissas
08858 !    and weights must be adjusted.  This can be done on the fly,
08859 !    or by calling this routine.
08860 !
08861 !    If the weight function W(X) is not 1, then the W vector will
08862 !    require further adjustment by the user.
08863 !
08864 !  Modified:
08865 !
08866 !    06 December 2000
08867 !
08868 !  Author:
08869 !
08870 !    John Burkardt
08871 !
08872 !  Parameters:
08873 !
08874 !    Input, double precision A, B, the endpoints of the definition interval.
08875 !
08876 !    Input, double precision C, D, the endpoints of the integration interval.
08877 !
08878 !    Input, integer NORDER, the number of abscissas and weights.
08879 !
08880 !    Input/output, double precision X(NORDER), W(NORDER), the abscissas
08881 !    and weights.
08882 !
08883   implicit none
08884 !
08885   integer norder
08886 !
08887   double precision a
08888   double precision b
08889   double precision c
08890   double precision d
08891   double precision w(norder)
08892   double precision x(norder)
08893 !
08894   x(1:norder) = ( ( b - x(1:norder) ) * c + ( x(1:norder) - a ) * d ) &
08895     / ( b - a )
08896 
08897   w(1:norder) = ( ( d - c ) / ( b - a ) ) * w(1:norder)
08898 
08899   return
08900 end
08901 subroutine summer ( func, norder, xtab, weight, result )
08902 !
08903 !*******************************************************************************
08904 !
08905 !! SUMMER carries out a quadrature rule over a single interval.
08906 !
08907 !
08908 !  Formula:
08909 !
08910 !    RESULT = SUM ( 1 <= I <= NORDER ) WEIGHT(I) * FUNC ( XTAB(I) )
08911 !
08912 !  Modified:
08913 !
08914 !    16 September 1998
08915 !
08916 !  Author:
08917 !
08918 !    John Burkardt
08919 !
08920 !  Parameters:
08921 !
08922 !    Input, external FUNC, the name of the FORTRAN function which
08923 !    evaluates the integrand.  The function must have the form
08924 !      double precision func ( x ).
08925 !
08926 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.
08927 !
08928 !    Input, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of the rule.
08929 !
08930 !    Input, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the rule.
08931 !
08932 !    Output, double precision RESULT, the approximate value of the integral.
08933 !
08934   implicit none
08935 !
08936   integer norder
08937 !
08938   double precision, external :: func
08939   integer i
08940   double precision result
08941   double precision weight(norder)
08942   double precision xtab(norder)
08943 !
08944   if ( norder < 1 ) then
08945     write ( *, '(a)' ) ' '
08946     write ( *, '(a)' ) 'SUMMER - Fatal error!'
08947     write ( *, '(a)' ) '  NORDER must be at least 1.'
08948     write ( *, '(a,i6)' ) '  The input value was NORDER = ', norder
08949     stop
08950   end if
08951 
08952   result = 0.0D+00
08953   do i = 1, norder
08954     result = result + weight(i) * func ( xtab(i) )
08955   end do
08956 
08957   return
08958 end
08959 subroutine summer_gk ( func, norderg, weightg, resultg, norderk, xtabk, &
08960   weightk, resultk )
08961 !
08962 !*******************************************************************************
08963 !
08964 !! SUMMER_GK carries out Gauss-Kronrod quadrature over a single interval.
08965 !
08966 !
08967 !  Note:
08968 !
08969 !    The abscissas for the Gauss-Legendre rule of order NORDERG are
08970 !    not required, since they are assumed to be the even-indexed
08971 !    entries of the corresponding Kronrod rule.
08972 !
08973 !  Modified:
08974 !
08975 !    16 September 1998
08976 !
08977 !  Author:
08978 !
08979 !    John Burkardt
08980 !
08981 !  Parameters:
08982 !
08983 !    Input, external FUNC, the name of the FORTRAN function which
08984 !    evaluates the integrand.  The function must have the form
08985 !      double precision func ( x ).
08986 !
08987 !    Input, integer NORDERG, the order of the Gauss-Legendre rule.
08988 !
08989 !    Input, double precision WEIGHTG(NORDERG), the weights of the
08990 !    Gauss-Legendre rule.
08991 !
08992 !    Output, double precision RESULTG, the approximate value of the
08993 !    integral, based on the Gauss-Legendre rule.
08994 !
08995 !    Input, integer NORDERK, the order of the Kronrod rule.  NORDERK
08996 !    must equal 2 * NORDERG + 1.
08997 !
08998 !    Input, double precision XTABK(NORDERK), the abscissas of the Kronrod rule.
08999 !
09000 !    Input, double precision WEIGHTK(NORDERK), the weights of the Kronrod rule.
09001 !
09002 !    Output, double precision RESULTK, the approximate value of the integral,
09003 !    based on the Kronrod rule.
09004 !
09005   implicit none
09006 !
09007   integer norderg
09008   integer norderk
09009 !
09010   double precision fk
09011   double precision, external :: func
09012   integer i
09013   double precision resultg
09014   double precision resultk
09015   double precision weightg(norderg)
09016   double precision weightk(norderk)
09017   double precision xtabk(norderk)
09018 !
09019   if ( norderk /= 2 * norderg + 1 ) then
09020     write ( *, '(a)' ) ' '
09021     write ( *, '(a)' ) 'SUMMER_GK - Fatal error!'
09022     write ( *, '(a)' ) '  NORDERK must equal 2 * NORDERG + 1.'
09023     write ( *, '(a,i6)' ) '  The input value was NORDERG = ', norderg
09024     write ( *, '(a,i6)' ) '  The input value was NORDERK = ', norderk
09025     stop
09026   end if
09027 
09028   resultg = 0.0D+00
09029   resultk = 0.0D+00
09030 
09031   do i = 1, norderk
09032 
09033     fk = func ( xtabk(i) )
09034 
09035     resultk = resultk + weightk(i) * fk
09036 
09037     if ( mod ( i, 2 ) == 0 )then
09038       resultg = resultg + weightg(i/2) * fk
09039     end if
09040 
09041   end do
09042 
09043   return
09044 end
09045 subroutine sum_sub ( func, a, b, nsub, norder, xlo, xhi, xtab, weight, result )
09046 !
09047 !*******************************************************************************
09048 !
09049 !! SUM_SUB carries out a composite quadrature rule.
09050 !
09051 !
09052 !  Discussion:
09053 !
09054 !    SUM_SUB assumes the original rule was written for [XLO,XHI].
09055 !
09056 !  Integration interval:
09057 !
09058 !    [ A, B ]
09059 !
09060 !  Integral to approximate:
09061 !
09062 !    Integral ( A <= X <= B ) F(X) dX
09063 !
09064 !  Modified:
09065 !
09066 !    06 December 2000
09067 !
09068 !  Author:
09069 !
09070 !    John Burkardt
09071 !
09072 !  Parameters:
09073 !
09074 !    Input, external FUNC, the name of the FORTRAN function which
09075 !    evaluates the integrand.  The function must have the form
09076 !      double precision func ( x ).
09077 !
09078 !    Input, double precision A, B, the lower and upper limits of integration.
09079 !
09080 !    Input, integer NSUB, the number of equal subintervals into
09081 !    which the finite interval (A,B) is to be subdivided for
09082 !    higher accuracy.  NSUB must be at least 1.
09083 !
09084 !    Input, integer NORDER, the order of the rule.
09085 !    NORDER must be at least 1.
09086 !
09087 !    Input, double precision XLO, XHI, the left and right endpoints of
09088 !    the interval over which the quadrature rule was defined.
09089 !
09090 !    Input, double precision XTAB(NORDER), the abscissas of a quadrature
09091 !    rule for the interval [XLO,XHI].
09092 !
09093 !    Input, double precision WEIGHT(NORDER), the weights of the quadrature rule.
09094 !
09095 !    Output, double precision RESULT, the approximate value of the integral.
09096 !
09097   implicit none
09098 !
09099   integer norder
09100 !
09101   double precision a
09102   double precision a_sub
09103   double precision b
09104   double precision b_sub
09105   double precision, external :: func
09106   double precision h
09107   integer i
09108   integer j
09109   integer nsub
09110   double precision quad_sub
09111   double precision result
09112   double precision result_sub
09113   double precision x
09114   double precision xhi
09115   double precision xlo
09116   double precision xmid
09117   double precision xtab(norder)
09118   double precision volume
09119   double precision volume_sub
09120   double precision weight(norder)
09121 !
09122   if ( a == b ) then
09123     result = 0.0D+00
09124     return
09125   end if
09126 
09127   if ( norder < 1 ) then
09128     write ( *, '(a)' ) ' '
09129     write ( *, '(a)' ) 'SUM_SUB - Fatal error!'
09130     write ( *, '(a,i6)' ) '  Nonpositive value of NORDER = ', norder
09131     stop
09132   end if
09133 
09134   if ( nsub < 1 ) then
09135     write ( *, '(a)' ) ' '
09136     write ( *, '(a)' ) 'SUM_SUB - Fatal error!'
09137     write ( *, '(a,i6)' ) '  Nonpositive value of NSUB = ', nsub
09138     stop
09139   end if
09140 
09141   if ( xlo == xhi ) then
09142     write ( *, '(a)' ) ' '
09143     write ( *, '(a)' ) 'SUM_SUB - Fatal error!'
09144     write ( *, '(a)' ) '  XLO = XHI.'
09145     stop
09146   end if
09147 
09148   volume = 0.0D+00
09149   result = 0.0D+00
09150 
09151   do j = 1, nsub
09152 
09153     a_sub = ( dble ( nsub - j + 1 ) * a + dble ( j - 1 ) * b ) / dble ( nsub )
09154     b_sub = ( dble ( nsub - j )     * a + dble ( j )     * b ) / dble ( nsub )
09155 
09156     quad_sub = 0.0D+00
09157     do i = 1, norder
09158       x = ( ( xhi - xtab(i) ) * a_sub + ( xtab(i) - xlo ) * b_sub ) &
09159         / ( xhi - xlo )
09160       quad_sub = quad_sub + weight(i) * func ( x )
09161     end do
09162 
09163     volume_sub = ( b - a ) / ( ( xhi - xlo ) * dble ( nsub ) )
09164     result_sub = quad_sub * volume_sub
09165 
09166     volume = volume + volume_sub
09167     result = result + result_sub
09168 
09169   end do
09170 
09171   return
09172 end
09173 subroutine sum_sub_gk ( func, a, b, nsub, norderg, weightg, resultg, norderk, &
09174   xtabk, weightk, resultk, error )
09175 !
09176 !*******************************************************************************
09177 !
09178 !! SUM_SUB_GK carries out a composite Gauss-Kronrod rule.
09179 !
09180 !
09181 !  Integration interval:
09182 !
09183 !    [ A, B ]
09184 !
09185 !  Integral to approximate:
09186 !
09187 !    Integral ( A <= X <= B ) F(X) dX
09188 !
09189 !  Approximate integral:
09190 !
09191 !    H = ( B - A ) / NSUB
09192 !    XMID(J) = A + 0.5 * H * REAL ( 2 * J - 1 )
09193 !
09194 !    Sum ( 1 <= J <= NSUB )
09195 !      Sum ( 1 <= I <= NORDERK )
09196 !        WEIGHTK(I) * F ( XMID(J) + 0.5 * H * XTABK(I) )
09197 !
09198 !  Note:
09199 !
09200 !    The Gauss-Legendre weights should be computed by LEGCOM or LEGSET.
09201 !    The Kronrod abscissas and weights should be computed by KRONSET.
09202 !
09203 !    The orders of the Gauss-Legendre and Kronrod rules must satisfy
09204 !    NORDERK = 2 * NORDERG + 1.
09205 !
09206 !    The Kronrod rule uses the abscissas of the Gauss-Legendre rule,
09207 !    plus more points, resulting in an efficient and higher order estimate.
09208 !
09209 !    The difference between the Gauss-Legendre and Kronrod estimates
09210 !    is taken as an estimate of the error in the approximation to the
09211 !    integral.
09212 !
09213 !  Modified:
09214 !
09215 !    15 September 1998
09216 !
09217 !  Author:
09218 !
09219 !    John Burkardt
09220 !
09221 !  Parameters:
09222 !
09223 !    Input, external FUNC, the name of the FORTRAN function which
09224 !    evaluates the integrand.  The function must have the form
09225 !      double precision func ( x ).
09226 !
09227 !    Input, double precision A, B, the lower and upper limits of integration.
09228 !
09229 !    Input, integer NSUB, the number of equal subintervals into
09230 !    which the finite interval (A,B) is to be subdivided for
09231 !    higher accuracy.  NSUB must be at least 1.
09232 !
09233 !    Input, integer NORDERG, the order of the Gauss-Legendre rule.
09234 !    NORDERG must be at least 1.
09235 !
09236 !    Input, double precision WEIGHTG(NORDERG), the weights of the
09237 !    Gauss-Legendre rule.
09238 !
09239 !    Output, double precision RESULTG, the approximate value of the
09240 !    integral based on the Gauss-Legendre rule.
09241 !
09242 !    Input, integer NORDERK, the order of the Kronrod rule.
09243 !    NORDERK must be at least 1.
09244 !
09245 !    Input, double precision XTABK(NORDERK), the abscissas of the
09246 !    Kronrod rule.
09247 !
09248 !    Input, double precision WEIGHTK(NORDERK), the weights of the
09249 !    Kronrod rule.
09250 !
09251 !    Output, double precision RESULTK, the approximate value of the
09252 !    integral based on the Kronrod rule.
09253 !
09254 !    Output, double precision ERROR, an estimate of the approximation
09255 !    error.  This is computed by taking the sum of the absolute values of
09256 !    the differences between the Gauss-Legendre and Kronrod rules
09257 !    over each subinterval.  This is usually a good estimate of
09258 !    the error in the value RESULTG.  The error in the Kronrod
09259 !    estimate RESULTK is usually much smaller.
09260 !
09261   implicit none
09262 !
09263   integer norderg
09264   integer norderk
09265 !
09266   double precision a
09267   double precision b
09268   double precision error
09269   double precision fk
09270   double precision, external :: func
09271   double precision h
09272   integer i
09273   integer j
09274   integer nsub
09275   double precision partg
09276   double precision partk
09277   double precision resultg
09278   double precision resultk
09279   double precision x
09280   double precision xmid
09281   double precision xtabk(norderk)
09282   double precision weightg(norderg)
09283   double precision weightk(norderk)
09284 !
09285   resultg = 0.0D+00
09286   resultk = 0.0D+00
09287   error = 0
09288 
09289   if ( a == b ) then
09290     return
09291   end if
09292 
09293   if ( norderk /= 2 * norderg + 1 ) then
09294     write ( *, '(a)' ) ' '
09295     write ( *, '(a)' ) 'SUM_SUB_GK - Fatal error!'
09296     write ( *, '(a)' ) '  NORDERK must equal 2 * NORDERG + 1.'
09297     write ( *, '(a,i6)' ) '  The input value was NORDERG = ', norderg
09298     write ( *, '(a,i6)' ) '  The input value was NORDERK = ', norderk
09299     stop
09300   end if
09301 
09302   h = ( b - a ) / dble ( nsub )
09303 
09304   do j = 1, nsub
09305 
09306     xmid = a + 0.5D0 * h * dble ( 2 * j - 1 )
09307 
09308     partg = 0.0D+00
09309     partk = 0.0D+00
09310 
09311     do i = 1, norderk
09312 
09313       x = xmid + 0.5D0 * h * xtabk(i)
09314       fk = func ( x )
09315       partk = partk + 0.5D0 * h * weightk(i) * fk
09316 
09317       if ( mod ( i, 2 ) == 0 ) then
09318         partg = partg + 0.5D0 * h * weightg(i/2) * fk
09319       end if
09320 
09321     end do
09322 
09323     resultg = resultg + partg
09324     resultk = resultk + partk
09325     error = error + abs ( partk - partg )
09326 
09327   end do
09328 
09329   return
09330 end
